working_hours_duration(start, end):\n    \"\"\"Calculate duration in working hours between two timestamps\"\"\"\n    if pd.isna(start) or pd.isna(end):\n        return 0\n    total_hours = 0\n    current = start\n    while current < end:\n        if current.weekday() >= 5:\n            current += timedelta(days=1)\n            current = current.replace(hour=WORK_START, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)\n            continue\n        day_start = current.replace(hour=WORK_START, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)\n        day_end = current.replace(hour=WORK_END, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)\n        if current < day_start:\n            current = day_start\n            continue\n        if current >= day_end:\n            current += timedelta(days=1)\n            current = current.replace(hour=WORK_START, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)\n            continue\n        segment_end = min(end, day_end)\n        total_hours += (segment_end - current).total_seconds() / 3600\n        current = day_end\n    return total_hours\n\ndef analyze():\n    employees, tasks, task_assignments, code_reviews, approvals, deployments, meetings, meeting_participants, messages, incidents, qa_tests, projects = load_data()\n    \n    emp_map = employees.set_index('employee_id').to_dict('index')\n    \n    scores = {}\n    for eid in employees['employee_id']:\n        scores[eid] = {\n            'delay_score': 0.0,\n            'overload_score': 0.0,\n            'blocking_score': 0.0,\n            'total_score': 0.0,\n            'task_delays': [],\n            'review_delays': [],\n            'approval_delays': [],\n        }\n    \n    # 1. Task assignment delays - how long after being assigned does an employee complete their work\n    # Group by task and look at sequential assignments to see if an employee causes gaps\n    for _, task in tasks.iterrows():\n        tid = task['task_id']\n        task_start = task['created_at']\n        \n        assignments = task_assignments[task_assignments['task_id'] == tid].sort_values('assigned_at')\n        if len(assignments) == 0:\n            continue\n        \n        task_total_duration = working_hours_duration(task_start, task['completed_at']) if pd.notna(task['completed_at']) else 0\n        \n        # Calculate expected duration based on complexity/risk\n        complexity = task.get('complexity_score', 3) or 3\n        risk = task.get('risk_score', 3) or 3\n        expected_hours = complexity * risk * 0.5  # rough baseline\n        \n        if task_total_duration > expected_hours * 3 and task_total_duration > 10:\n            # Task took much longer than expected - find who delayed it\n            pass\n        \n        # Look at each assignment step\n        prev_unassigned = task_start\n        for _, assn in assignments.iterrows():\n            emp_id = assn['employee_id']\n            assigned_at = assn['assigned_at']\n            unassigned_at = assn['unassigned_at'] if pd.notna(assn['unassigned_at']) else task['completed_at']\n            \n            if pd.isna(unassigned_at):\n                continue\n            \n            # Gap between previous step's completion and this step's start\n            gap = working_hours_duration(prev_unassigned, assigned_at)\n            \n            # Time this employee actually took\n            work_time = working_hours_duration(assigned_at, unassigned_at)\n            \n            # Expected time based on role\n            role_expected = {\n                'triage': 0.5, 'investigate': 2, 'implement': 4, 'code_reviewer': 1,\n                'security_reviewer': 1, 'approver': 0.5, 'deployer': 0.5,\n                'owner': 6, 'verify': 1, 'tester': 2, 'design': 3,\n                'architecture_reviewer': 1\n            }.get(assn['assignment_role'], 2)\n            \n            if work_time > role_expected * 4 and work_time > 4:\n                # This employee took too long on this assignment\n                delay = work_time - role_expected\n                scores[emp_id]['task_delays'].append({\n                    'task_id': tid,\n                    'delay': delay,\n                    'work_time': work_time,\n                    'expected': role_expected\n                })\n            \n            # Check for gaps waiting for this employee\n            if gap > 4:\n                # Task was waiting for someone before this employee could start\n                pass\n            \n            prev_unassigned = unassigned_at\n    \n    # 2. Code review delays\n    for _, review in code_reviews.iterrows():\n        reviewer = review['reviewer_id']\n        req_at = review['requested_at']\n        comp_at = review['completed_at']\n        \n        if pd.notna(req_at) and pd.notna(comp_at):\n            duration = working_hours_duration(req_at, comp_at)\n            if duration > 4:\n                scores[reviewer]['review_delays'].append({\n                    'task_id': review['task_id'],\n                    'delay': duration - 1,  # expected ~1 hour\n                    'duration': duration\n                })\n    \n    # 3. Approval delays\n    for _, approval in approvals.iterrows():\n        approver = approval['approver_id']\n        req_at = approval['requested_at']\n        res_at = approval['resolved_at']\n        \n        if pd.notna(req_at) and pd.notna(res_at):\n            duration = working_hours_duration(req_at, res_at)\n            if duration > 2:\n                scores[approver]['approval_delays'].append({\n                    'task_id': approval['task_id'],\n                    'delay': duration - 0.5,  # expected half hour\n                    'duration': duration\n                })\n    \n    # 4. Meeting load per employee\n    meeting_emp_time = {}\n    for _, mp in meeting_participants.iterrows():\n        eid = mp['employee_id']\n        mid = mp['meeting_id']\n        meeting = meetings[meetings['meeting_id'] == mid]\n        if len(meeting) == 0:\n            continue\n        meeting = meeting.iloc[0]\n        dur = working_hours_duration(meeting['start_time'], meeting['end_time'])\n        if eid not in meeting_emp_time:\n            meeting_emp_time[eid] = 0\n        meeting_emp_time[eid] += dur\n    \n    # 5. Message volume per employee\n    msg_count = {}\n    for _, msg in messages.iterrows():\n        for eid in [msg['sender_id'], msg['receiver_id']]:\n            if eid not in msg_count:\n                msg_count[eid] = 0\n            msg_count[eid] += 1\n    \n    # 6. Concurrent task load - tasks assigned at same time\n    emp_concurrent = {}\n    for _, assn in task_assignments.iterrows():\n        eid = assn['employee_id']\n        if pd.notna(assn['assigned_at']) and pd.notna(assn['unassigned_at']):\n            if eid not in emp_concurrent:\n                emp_concurrent[eid] = []\n            emp_concurrent[eid].append((assn['assigned_at'], assn['unassigned_at']))\n    \n    max_concurrent = {}\n    for eid, periods in emp_concurrent.items():\n        if len(periods) < 5:\n            continue\n        # Sample at various times\n        max_c = 0\n        for i in range(len(periods)):\n            t = periods[i][0]\n            count = sum(1 for s, e in periods if s <= t <= e)\n            max_c = max(max_c, count)\n        max_concurrent[eid] = max_c\n    \n    # 7. Identify employees with highest delays\n    all_metrics = {}\n    \n    for eid in scores:\n        total_delay = sum(d['delay'] for d in scores[eid]['task_delays']) + \\\n                      sum(d['delay'] for d in scores[eid]['review_delays']) + \\\n                      sum(d['delay'] for d in scores[eid]['approval_delays'])\n        \n        num_delays = len(scores[eid]['task_delays']) + len(scores[eid]['review_delays']) + len(scores[eid]['approval_delays'])\n        \n        meeting_hrs = meeting_emp_time.get(eid, 0)\n        msgs = msg_count.get(eid, 0)\n        concurrent = max_concurrent.get(eid, 0)\n        \n        role = emp_map[eid]['seniority_level'] if eid in emp_map else 'unknown'\n        dept = emp_map[eid]['department'] if eid in emp_map else 'unknown'\n        \n        all_metrics[eid] = {\n            'role': role,\n            'department': dept,\n            'total_delay_hours': total_delay,\n            'num_delays': num_delays,\n            'meeting_hours': meeting_hrs,\n            'messages': msgs,\n            'max_concurrent_tasks': concurrent,\n        }\n    \n    # 8. Identify incidents linked to tasks where employee was involved\n    emp_incident_count = {}\n    for _, inc in incidents.iterrows():\n        tid = inc['related_task_id']\n        sev = inc['severity']\n        owner = inc['owner_id']\n        if owner not in emp_incident_count:\n            emp_incident_count[owner] = 0\n        emp_incident_count[owner] += 1\n        \n        # Also check if resolved_at is very late (delayed)\n        if pd.notna(inc['created_at']) and pd.notna(inc['resolved_at']):\n            resolution_time = working_hours_duration(inc['created_at'], inc['resolved_at'])\n            if resolution_time > 40:\n                if owner not in emp_incident_count:\n                    emp_incident_count[owner] = 0\n                emp_incident_count[owner] += 1\n    \n    for eid in all_metrics:\n        all_metrics[eid]['incident_count'] = emp_incident_count.get(eid, 0)\n    \n    # Compute Z-scores for each metric\n    metrics_df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(all_metrics, orient='index')\n    \n    # Fill NaN\n    metrics_df = metrics_df.fillna(0)\n    \n    # Z-score normalize relevant metrics\n    for col in ['total_delay_hours', 'num_delays', 'meeting_hours', 'messages', 'max_concurrent_tasks', 'incident_count']:\n        if col in metrics_df.columns:\n            mean = metrics_df[col].mean()\n            std = metrics_df[col].std()\n            if std > 0:\n                metrics_df[f'z_{col}'] = (metrics_df[col] - mean) / std\n            else:\n                metrics_df[f'z_{col}'] = 0\n    \n    # Combine into a composite score\n    metrics_df['composite'] = (\n        metrics_df.get('z_total_delay_hours', 0) * 0.30 +\n        metrics_df.get('z_num_delays', 0) * 0.20 +\n        metrics_df.get('z_meeting_hours', 0) * 0.15 +\n        metrics_df.get('z_messages', 0) * 0.05 +\n        metrics_df.get('z_max_concurrent_tasks', 0) * 0.15 +\n        metrics_df.get('z_incident_count', 0) * 0.15\n    )\n    \n    # Sort by composite score descending\n    metrics_df = metrics_df.sort_values('composite', ascending=False)\n    \n    # Print top candidates\n    print(\"Top potential bottleneck employees:\")\n    print(metrics_df.head(30).to_string())\n    \n    # Select employees with composite score > 1.5 (significantly above average)\n    threshold = 1.8\n    candidates = metrics_df[metrics_df['composite'] > threshold].index.tolist()\n    \n    print(f\"\\n\\nSelected {len(candidates)} bottleneck employees with composite > {threshold}:\")\n    print(candidates)\n    print(metrics_df.loc[candidates].to_string())\n    \n    # Let's also look at the specific patterns more carefully\n    return candidates, metrics_df\n\ndef analyze_v2(employees, tasks, task_assignments, code_reviews, approvals, deployments, \n               meetings, meeting_participants, messages, incidents, qa_tests, projects):\n    \n    emp_map = employees.set_index('employee_id').to_dict('index')\n    all_employee_ids = employees['employee_id'].tolist()\n    \n    scores = {eid: 0.0 for eid in all_employee_ids}\n    reasons = {eid: [] for eid in all_employee_ids}\n    \n    def wh_hours(start, end):\n        if pd.isna(start) or pd.isna(end):\n            return 0\n        return working_hours_duration(start, end)\n    \n    # --- Approach: Track the flow of each task through the pipeline ---\n    # For each task, identify who caused the longest delays\n    \n    task_flow_delays = {}  # emp_id -> total delay hours they caused\n    \n    for _, task in tasks.iterrows():\n        tid = task['task_id']\n        task_start = task['created_at']\n        task_end = task['completed_at'] if pd.notna(task['completed_at']) else None\n        \n        if task_end is None:\n            continue\n            \n        assignments = task_assignments[task_assignments['task_id'] == tid].sort_values('assigned_at')\n        if len(assignments) == 0:\n            continue\n        \n        # Total task duration\n        total_dur = wh_hours(task_start, task_end)\n        \n        # Calculate expected task duration based on complexity\n        complexity = task.get('complexity_score', 3) or 3\n        risk = task.get('risk_score', 3) or 3\n        priority = task.get('priority', 'medium')\n        prio_mult = {'critical': 0.5, 'high': 0.7, 'medium': 1.0, 'low': 1.5}.get(priority, 1.0)\n        \n        expected_dur = complexity * 0.5 + risk * 0.3 * prio_mult\n        \n        # If task took much longer than expected, find who delayed it\n        if total_dur > expected_dur * 2:\n            # Look at each step of the pipeline\n            prev_time = task_start\n            \n            for _, assn in assignments.iterrows():\n                eid = assn['employee_id']\n                assigned_at = assn['assigned_at']\n                unassigned_at = assn['unassigned_at'] if pd.notna(assn['unassigned_at']) else task_end\n                \n                # Gap before this employee could start (waiting time)\n                wait_time = wh_hours(prev_time, assigned_at)\n                \n                # Time this employee spent\n                work_time = wh_hours(assigned_at, unassigned_at)\n                \n                # Expected time for this role\n                role_expected = {\n                    'triage': 0.25, 'investigate': 1, 'implement': 3, 'code_reviewer': 0.5,\n                    'security_reviewer': 0.5, 'approver': 0.25, 'deployer': 0.25,\n                    'owner': 4, 'verify': 0.5, 'tester': 1, 'design': 2,\n                    'architecture_reviewer': 0.5\n                }.get(assn['assignment_role'], 1)\n                \n                # Adjust expected for task complexity\n                role_expected = role_expected * (1 + complexity * 0.1)\n                \n                # If work takes too long, employee is a bottleneck\n                if work_time > role_expected * 2:\n                    delay = work_time - role_expected\n                    if eid not in task_flow_delays:\n                        task_flow_delays[eid] = 0\n                    task_flow_delays[eid] += delay\n                    reasons[eid].append(f\"task_{tid}_work_delay:{delay:.1f}h\")\n                \n                # If there's a large gap between this employee's completion and the next step,\n                # also attribute some of that to the current employee (they might not have handed off properly)\n                # Actually, that gap is waiting for the next person, so attribute to the next person\n                prev_time = unassigned_at\n    \n    # --- Code Review delays ---\n    review_delays = {}\n    for _, review in code_reviews.iterrows():\n        eid = review['reviewer_id']\n        dur = wh_hours(review['requested_at'], review['completed_at'])\n        expected = 0.5\n        if dur > expected * 3 and dur > 1:\n            delay = dur - expected\n            if eid not in review_delays:\n                review_delays[eid] = 0\n            review_delays[eid] += delay\n            reasons[eid].append(f\"review_delay:{delay:.1f}h\")\n    \n    # --- Approval delays ---\n    approval_delays = {}\n    for _, approval in approvals.iterrows():\n        eid = approval['approver_id']\n        dur = wh_hours(approval['requested_at'], approval['resolved_at'])\n        expected = 0.25\n        if dur > expected * 4 and dur > 1:\n            delay = dur - expected\n            if eid not in approval_delays:\n                approval_delays[eid] = 0\n            approval_delays[eid] += delay\n            reasons[eid].append(f\"approval_delay:{delay:.1f}h\")\n    \n    # --- Meetings: total hours in meetings ---\n    meeting_hours = {}\n    for _, mp in meeting_participants.iterrows():\n        eid = mp['employee_id']\n        mid = mp['meeting_id']\n        meeting = meetings[meetings['meeting_id'] == mid]\n        if len(meeting) == 0:\n            continue\n        meeting = meeting.iloc[0]\n        dur = wh_hours(meeting['start_time'], meeting['end_time'])\n        if eid not in meeting_hours:\n            meeting_hours[eid] = 0\n        meeting_hours[eid] += dur\n    \n    # --- Concurrent task load ---\n    task_periods = {}\n    for _, assn in task_assignments.iterrows():\n        eid = assn['employee_id']\n        if pd.notna(assn['assigned_at']) and pd.notna(assn['unassigned_at']):\n            if eid not in task_periods:\n                task_periods[eid] = []\n            task_periods[eid].append((assn['assigned_at'], assn['unassigned_at']))\n    \n    max_concurrent = {}\n    for eid, periods in task_periods.items():\n        if len(periods) < 3:\n            continue\n        times = []\n        for s, e in periods:\n            times.append((s, 1))\n            times.append((e, -1))\n        times.sort()\n        cur = 0\n        mx = 0\n        for _, delta in times:\n            cur += delta\n            mx = max(mx, cur)\n        max_concurrent[eid] = mx\n    \n    # --- Messages ---\n    msg_counts = {}\n    for _, msg in messages.iterrows():\n        for eid in [msg['sender_id'], msg['receiver_id']]:\n            msg_counts[eid] = msg_counts.get(eid, 0) + 1\n    \n    # --- Incident involvement ---\n    incident_severity = {}\n    for _, inc in incidents.iterrows():\n        eid = inc['owner_id']\n        sev_points = {'critical': 3, 'high': 2, 'medium': 1, 'low': 0.5}.get(inc['severity'], 1)\n        incident_severity[eid] = incident_severity.get(eid, 0) + sev_points\n    \n    # --- QA Test failures (poor performance) ---\n    qa_failures = {}\n    for _, qt in qa_tests.iterrows():\n        eid = qt['tester_id']\n        if qt['test_result'] == 'failed':\n            qa_failures[eid] = qa_failures.get(eid, 0) + 1\n    \n    # --- Now compute composite score ---\n    metrics_list = []\n    for eid in all_employee_ids:\n        emp = emp_map.get(eid, {})\n        task_delay = task_flow_delays.get(eid, 0)\n        review_delay = review_delays.get(eid, 0)\n        approval_delay = approval_delays.get(eid, 0)\n        total_delay = task_delay + review_delay + approval_delay\n        mhrs = meeting_hours.get(eid, 0)\n        msgs = msg_counts.get(eid, 0)\n        conc = max_concurrent.get(eid, 0)\n        inc_sev = incident_severity.get(eid, 0)\n        qa_fail = qa_failures.get(eid, 0)\n        \n        metrics_list.append({\n            'employee_id': eid,\n            'role': emp.get('seniority_level', 'unknown'),\n            'department': emp.get('department', 'unknown'),\n            'total_delay': total_delay,\n            'task_delay': task_delay,\n            'review_delay': review_delay,\n            'approval_delay': approval_delay,\n            'meeting_hours': mhrs,\n            'messages': msgs,\n            'max_concurrent': conc,\n            'incident_severity': inc_sev,\n            'qa_failures': qa_fail,\n        })\n    \n    mdf = pd.DataFrame(metrics_list)\n    mdf = mdf.fillna(0)\n    \n    # Z-score normalization\n    score_cols = ['total_delay', 'meeting_hours', 'messages', 'max_concurrent', 'incident_severity']\n    for col in score_cols:\n        if col in mdf.columns:\n            mean = mdf[col].mean()\n            std = mdf[col].std()\n            if std > 0:\n                mdf[f'z_{col}'] = (mdf[col] - mean) / std\n            else:\n                mdf[f'z_{col}'] = 0\n    \n    mdf['qa_fail_z'] = (mdf['qa_failures'] - mdf['qa_failures'].mean()) / mdf['qa_failures'].std() if mdf['qa_failures'].std() > 0 else 0\n    \n    # Composite: weight delays heavily, then overload indicators\n    mdf['composite'] = (\n        mdf['z_total_delay'] * 0.35 +\n        mdf['z_meeting_hours'] * 0.15 +\n        mdf['z_max_concurrent'] * 0.15 +\n        mdf['z_incident_severity'] * 0.15 +\n        mdf['qa_fail_z'] * 0.10 +\n        mdf['z_messages'] * 0.10\n    )\n    \n    mdf = mdf.sort_values('composite', ascending=False)\n    \n    print(\"\\n\\n===== ANALYSIS V2 =====\")\n    print(\"Top 40 employees by composite score:\")\n    for i, row in mdf.head(40).iterrows():\n        print(f\"  Emp {int(row['employee_id']):3d} | {row['role']:8s} | {row['department']:15s} | \"\n              f\"Delay:{row['total_delay']:6.1f}h | Meet:{row['meeting_hours']:5.1f}h | \"\n              f\"Conc:{row['max_concurrent']:2.0f} | Inc:{row['incident_severity']:4.1f} | \"\n              f\"Msgs:{row['messages']:4.0f} | QA:{row['qa_failures']:2.0f} | \"\n              f\"Comp:{row['composite']:.3f}\")\n    \n    return mdf\n\ndef main():\n    (employees, tasks, task_assignments, code_reviews, approvals, deployments, \n     meetings, meeting_participants, messages, incidents, qa_tests, projects) = load_data()\n    \n    mdf = analyze_v2(employees, tasks, task_assignments, code_reviews, approvals, deployments, \n                     meetings, meeting_participants, messages, incidents, qa_tests, projects)\n    \n    # Select candidates\n    # Look for the natural break\n    sorted_vals = mdf['composite'].values\n    \n    # Threshold: top employees with significant composite score\n    threshold = 1.5\n    candidates = mdf[mdf['composite'] > threshold]['employee_id'].tolist()\n    \n    print(f\"\\n\\nCandidates with composite > {threshold}: {candidates}\")\n    \n    # Let's also analyze the top decile\n    top_decile = mdf.head(max(len(mdf)//10, 10))\n    print(f\"\\nTop decile ({len(top_decile)} employees):\")\n    for i, row in top_decile.iterrows():\n        print(f\"  Emp {int(row['employee_id']):3d} | {row['role']:8s} | {row['department']:15s} | Comp:{row['composite']:.3f}\")\n    \n    # Additional analysis: who has the most \"blocked\" tasks waiting on them\n    # Look at gaps between task steps\n    task_blocks = {}\n    for _, task in tasks.iterrows():\n        tid = task['task_id']\n        assignments = task_assignments[task_assignments['task_id'] == tid].sort_values('assigned_at')\n        if len(assignments) < 2:\n            continue\n        \n        for i in range(1, len(assignments)):\n            prev = assignments.iloc[i-1]\n            curr = assignments.iloc[i]\n            \n            prev_end = prev['unassigned_at'] if pd.notna(prev['unassigned_at']) else None\n            curr_start = curr['assigned_at']\n            \n            if prev_end is not None:\n                gap = wh_hours(prev_end, curr_start)\n                if gap > 4:\n                    # The person who was supposed to come after prev_end is the one who's blocking\n                    # Actually, the gap is between prev_end and curr_start, meaning the next person\n                    # (curr employee) took a long time to start after previous step ended\n                    blocker = curr['employee_id']\n                    task_blocks[blocker] = task_blocks.get(blocker, 0) + gap\n    \n    print(\"\\n\\nTop blockers (by gap between task steps):\")\n    sorted_blockers = sorted(task_blocks.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    for eid, gap in sorted_blockers[:20]:\n        print(f\"  Emp {eid:3d} | Wait gap: {gap:.1f}h\")\n    \n    # wh_hours(start, end):\n    if pd.isna(start) or pd.isna(end):\n        return 0\n    total_hours = 0.0\n    current = start\n    while current < end:\n        if current.weekday() >= 5:\n
